    <script>
        // Sticky Header ao rolar a página (apenas desktop xl)
        const stickyHeader = document.getElementById('sticky-header');
        const mainHeader = document.getElementById('main-header');

        if (stickyHeader && window.innerWidth >= 1280) {
            let lastScrollTop = 0;
            let headerHeight = mainHeader ? mainHeader.offsetHeight : 0;

            window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
                const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

                // Mostra o sticky header quando rolar mais que a altura do header principal
                if (scrollTop > headerHeight && scrollTop > lastScrollTop) {
                    // Rolando para baixo
                    stickyHeader.classList.remove('-translate-y-full');
                    stickyHeader.classList.add('translate-y-0');
                } else if (scrollTop <= 100) {
                    // Próximo ao topo
                    stickyHeader.classList.add('-translate-y-full');
                    stickyHeader.classList.remove('translate-y-0');
                }

                lastScrollTop = scrollTop;
            });
        }

        // Navbar mobile
        const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
        const navbarButton = document.querySelector('.navbar-button');
        const navbarCloseButton = document.querySelector('.navbar-close-button');
        const iconMenu = navbarButton.querySelector('.icon-menu');
        const iconClose = navbarButton.querySelector('.icon-close');
        const backdrop = document.querySelector('.backdrop');

        const toggleNavbar = () => {
            navbar.classList.toggle('hidden');
            backdrop.classList.toggle('hidden');
            iconMenu.classList.toggle('!hidden');
            iconClose.classList.toggle('!hidden');
            $('body').toggleClass('overflow-hidden');
        };

        const closeNavbar = () => {
            navbar.classList.add('hidden');
            backdrop.classList.add('hidden');
            iconMenu.classList.remove('!hidden');
            iconClose.classList.add('!hidden');
            $('body').removeClass('overflow-hidden');
        };

        navbarButton.addEventListener('click', toggleNavbar);

        // Fecha ao clicar no button
        navbarCloseButton.addEventListener('click', closeNavbar);

        // Fecha ao clicar fora
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (
                !navbar.contains(e.target) &&
                !navbarButton.contains(e.target) &&
                !navbar.classList.contains('hidden')
            ) {
                closeNavbar();
            }
        });


        // Search form mobile
        const searchForm = document.querySelector('.search-form-mobile');
        const searchButton = document.querySelector('.search-button');
        const searchButtonClose = document.querySelector('.search-button-close');

        const toggleSearchForm = () => {
            searchForm.classList.toggle('hidden');
        };

        const closeSearchForm = () => {
            searchForm.classList.add('hidden');
        };

        searchButton.addEventListener('click', toggleSearchForm);


        searchButtonClose.addEventListener('click', closeSearchForm);
    </script>
